\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Enumeration of valid key mods (possibly O\-R'd together). \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\subsection{Detailed Description}
Defines constants which identify keyboard keys and modifiers.

\subsubsection[{S\-D\-L\-K\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-M\-A\-S\-K}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define S\-D\-L\-K\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-M\-A\-S\-K~(1$<$$<$30)}}\label{_s_d_l__keycode_8h_ad1ff7a791f8bc7b5c16cd89cf24fa927}


\subsection{Typedef Documentation}
\hypertarget{_s_d_l__keycode_8h_ae9265f064f13f0f74dfca26a67875171}{\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-keycode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-keycode.\-h}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Keycode@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Keycode}}
\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Keycode@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Keycode}!SDL_keycode.h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-keycode.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Keycode}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf Sint32} {\bf S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Keycode}}}\label{_s_d_l__keycode_8h_ae9265f064f13f0f74dfca26a67875171}


The S\-D\-L virtual key representation. 

Values of this type are used to represent keyboard keys using the current layout of the keyboard. These values include Unicode values representing the unmodified character that would be generated by pressing the key, or an S\-D\-L\-K\-\_\-$\ast$ constant for those keys that do not generate characters.
